Special Article

Review and Prospects of the Pacific International Society (Continued 2) Bin 61

(II) Origin of the Pacific International Society and Overview of the First and Second Conferences

The reason for organizing the Pacific International Society is that, as individuals, citizens can discuss the crux of international relations between countries along the Pacific coast and seek mutual understanding between the countries and peoples of the Pacific in order to promote international amity and, further, to seek permanent world peace as the initial intention. In the society's organizational law, the origin of its establishment was briefly described, stating, "To study the situation of the peoples of the Pacific and improve their mutual relations as the goal." In the "Pacific National Relations Discussion Conference" published by the society in September 1928, it also stated, "This society possesses a kind of driving force to study and interpret the ideas, culture, and systems of the Pacific countries through private hands, and to examine and remedy the conflicts between countries and peoples, and to promote their mutual understanding and respect for culture." It also stated, "In order to achieve the above objectives, the society enjoys the benefits of scientific research, cooperates sincerely, explores each other, and is not bound by official attitudes or limited by diplomatic situations. Therefore, the society is an organization of the people, not a combination of governments. What we pay attention to is also searching for the basis for maintaining peace in the Pacific, and exchanging opinions between countries and peoples with a frank and sincere attitude, and interpreting this basis." Judging from what is declared in words, the initiation of the society, in the sense of international peace, can be regarded as an international group promoting peace and a pioneering effort of national organizations in the international community after the European War. At the same time, it can also be regarded as a kind of national diplomacy that can seek mutual understanding between nations with a frank attitude in order to break the dangerous situation in the Pacific, truly opening a new era in international relations. Its initial intention can indeed be described as most beautiful and perfect.

The initiation of the Pacific International Society began with people in Christianity. After the end of the European War, there was a proposal to convene the YMCA of various Pacific countries in Honolulu. The scope was then expanded, changing to a convocation of Christian churches in the Pacific countries. Subsequently, the boundaries of the church were broken, changing again to a purely national conference. It was first advocated by important leaders in the business and academic circles of Honolulu, who consulted with scholars and celebrities from other related countries to initiate it. The first conference was held in Honolulu on July 1, 1925. The second conference was held in Honolulu on July 15, 1927. The third conference was held in Kyoto, Japan on October 28, 1929.

As for the international organization of the society, its highest authority is the Pacific Council, which is composed of one representative from each of the participating countries' councils in the Pacific. Next is the General Secretariat, which has a Secretary-General, and several secretaries in the Research Department, Conference Department, and Report Department. Next is the International Research Committee, which is composed of representatives of research members from the councils of the participating countries. As for the organization of the participating countries, it is called the National Councils of the Pacific National Relations Conference, which has the power of autonomy and equal power in deciding motions and procedures at international conferences. The entire organizational system is listed in the table below.

The origin and organization of the society are briefly described above. Now, a brief table is specially listed to provide an overview of the first and second conferences of the society, as follows.

Number First Conference Second Conference

Name Pacific National Conference, later renamed Pacific National Relations Conference Pacific National Relations Conference

Date July 1 to 15, 1925 July 15 to 28, 1927

Participating Countries Representatives from nine locations including China, Japan, the United States, Canada, Australia, New Zealand, Hawaii, and Little Luzon Representatives from Australia, Canada, China, the United Kingdom, Hawaii, Japan, Korea, New Zealand, the Philippines, and the United States, totaling 136 people

Chinese Representatives Luo Youjie, Wang Jiyu, Wen Shizhen, Gu Ziren, Chen Da, Chen Liting, Yan Yangchu, Ouyang Xinong, Li Shaochang, Lin Guofang, and 2 others Bao Mingqian, Chen Liting, Hao Boyang, Hong Ye, Gu Ziren, Li Shaochang, Liu Hongsheng, Lin Guofang, Niu Huisheng, Niu Xuheng, Wang Liaofengxian, Huang Fumin, Yu Rizhang, Chen Hengzhe, and 1 other

Important Issues The "Extraterritoriality," "Tariff Autonomy," and "Overseas Chinese Issues" proposed by the Chinese representatives and the "Development of Industry" proposed by foreigners were the main issues of this conference. The "Tariff Autonomy" and "Extraterritoriality" of China and the recovery of the Shanghai International Settlement were the focus of discussions at this conference. Other issues such as education, immigration, labor, and the new diplomacy of the Pacific were also discussed in detail. Discussion Situation (1) Germany, Austria, Russia and other countries all felt that extraterritoriality was no longer necessary. However, a few countries still argued that extraterritoriality could only be abolished when China's legal system became effective and China had a strong central government. (2) The participants felt that tariff autonomy and increased tax rates were necessary for our country. The American representative was the most sympathetic.

(3) The proposals of our country's representatives were fully adopted on the issue of overseas Chinese (4) On the issue of industry, it was unanimously advocated that respect for China's sovereignty and humanity should be regarded as reasonable investment so that China's industry could be fully developed

(1) Unanimously agreed in principle to China's tariff autonomy. However, there were still restrictions on implementation. As for the attitudes of various countries, they were not consistent. The United Kingdom seemed more willing to recognize it, while the United States and Japan both took treaty revision as a prerequisite. (2) There were two suggestions for solving the problem of consular jurisdiction. One was an excessive plan that could be implemented immediately, and the other was a plan to be adopted immediately when the official government of China was established. These plans were quite detailed. (3) Regarding the recovery of the Shanghai International Settlement, it was advocated that the Chinese government should appoint a Chinese municipal administrative authority for Greater Shanghai to be responsible for the administrative responsibilities of all public municipal affairs in the existing six districts (Nanshi French Concession International Settlement Jiangwan Zhabei Wusong). Other matters, such as the equal number of Chinese and non-Chinese directors in the International Settlement and the mayor in the International Settlement being elected by the board of directors, were also discussed in detail.

Observing the table on the right, it can be seen that the society attaches great importance to various issues in our country. Representatives from various countries were also able to make fair remarks during discussions. However, because Korea opposed Japan's tyrannical policy of aggression against Korea in the first conference, it was eventually excluded from the conference. The American representatives attended the meeting with a large majority of twenty-eight people, while the representatives of Little Luzon were only three. As for the requests of North Borneo and the Dutch East Indies to join being rejected, and no representatives from Taiwan and Singapore participating, all of these are major shortcomings of the society. As the society aims to promote national friendship and political understanding, it should be inclusive and treat all equally. With a fair and sincere attitude, an objective exploration of various issues can contribute to the friendship between Pacific countries and promote world peace. (To be continued)

Important News

Zhang Zuoxiang Suddenly Arrives in Beiping 62

Stays in Beiping for One Night and Immediately Returns to Shenyang

Talks About the Truth of the Wanbaoshan Case When Passing Through Tianjin

Beiping Correspondence: Zhang Zuoxiang, who is sitting in Shenyang on behalf of Zhang Xueliang, believes that after the Wanbaoshan Incident in Changchun, the Japanese side increased the number of police teams to assist the Koreans, and the situation is becoming increasingly serious, and negotiations may expand. It is necessary to present the truth to Zhang Xueliang and negotiate the response policy. Therefore, he left Shenyang on the 6th to enter the customs. He arrived in Beiping at 10 am on the 7th. After getting off the train, he went to the Beijing Hotel to rest. However, because he had just unloaded his luggage and was busy with official duties, he did not receive any visitors. That night, he went to the Peking Union Medical College Hospital to visit Zhang Xueliang. After meeting each other, Zhang Xueliang was very pleased and said that he had something to discuss and that his arrival was excellent. The funeral of the Grand Marshal was originally scheduled for October, but because I have not yet recovered and everything is not ready, it may be too late to hold the funeral in October. It is proposed to postpone it to December.

During the period, I should ask you to preside over the postponement. I have just recovered from a serious illness and need time to recuperate. I will not be able to return to Shenyang in the shortest time. If there are no important official matters in Jilin, please stay in Shenyang to sit in town. After listening to the words, Zhang Zuoxiang agreed one by one and then chatted for a few words before resigning. Because the doctor forbade him to talk too much, the Wanbaoshan Incident was not reported in person. According to Rong Mengmei, the secretary of Zhang, the biggest purpose of Chairman Zhang's entry into the customs this time was only to visit the vice commander's illness. The day before yesterday, he went to the Peking Union Medical College Hospital and saw that the vice commander was in good spirits. The talking time was only three minutes according to the doctor's instructions. The vice commander first thanked Chairman Zhang for his long-distance presence. The Wanbaoshan Incident was not as serious as the foreign propaganda. As of the time when the chairman and I entered the customs, the Japanese in Changchun County had shot at domestic farmers to demonstrate, but there were no casualties or expansion. Chairman Zhang did not report this matter when he saw the vice commander. At noon on the 8th, Mr. Zhang went to Wan Fulin's private residence for lunch. Yu Xuezhong, Wang Shuhan, Wang Shuchang, Ji Yiqiao, Zhang Xueming, etc. were all present. During the banquet, they discussed the Wanbaoshan Incident and important issues of Northeast diplomacy, and roughly made considerable decisions. At about 1 pm, they went to the Peking Union Medical College Hospital again with Wan Fulin, Zhang Xueming, Ji Yiqiao, Wang Shuchang, etc. to report to Zhang Xueliang and bid farewell. At 4:40 pm, they went to the East Railway Station to take a special train back to Shenyang. All the entourage

Page 11

Receive Important News 63

And all the guards, more than a hundred people, guarded along the way. Wan Fulin, Yu Xuezhong, Wang Shuchang, Ji Yiqiao, Zhang Xueming, etc. all went to the station to see them off. Yu Xuezhong and others originally scheduled a public banquet for Mr. Zhang on the evening of the 8th. Mr. Zhang had no time to attend the banquet and hurriedly returned east. Its significance can be imagined.

Tianjin Correspondence: On the afternoon of the 8th, Zhang Zuoxiang returned to Liaoning from Ping. At 8 o'clock, the train arrived at Tianjin East Station. Those who welcomed him at the station included Wang Yuke, He Yufang, Yao Hong, Zou Shangyou, Deng Qinglan, and Wang Yimin, the director of the Public Security Bureau. After the car stopped, Mr. Zhang got out of the car and briefly greeted the welcomers. The reporter asked for an interview and inquired about the truth of the Wanbaoshan Incident and the response policy. Mr. Zhang said that the truth of the matter was not as serious as the newspaper propaganda. Its origin was because a Chinese man, Hao Yongde, colluded with Li Zhaohe and others who had registered as Koreans in Changchun County to rent 500 mu of land and diverted water from the Yitong River to dig waterways to grow rice fields. The excavated waterway was 25 miles long, passing through nine villages, one zhang deep and about three or four zhang wide, occupying a lot of land from the county people. Therefore, the county people resolutely opposed this matter. However, the Koreans still ignored it, and the Japanese consul in Changchun Tian Dynasty increased the number of Japanese police to protect the Korean Qiaos in their excavation work. For a time, it aroused resentment among the people, and the Chinese police also stepped forward to protect our people. On the 20th of last month, when the Koreans were working on excavating the waterway, the Chinese gathered a crowd and filled the ditch with soil, filling it for about several miles. For a time, the atmosphere was tense. The Koreans clashed with our people, and the Japanese police also helped the Koreans open fire. Our people and the police team retreated into the ditch and fired back. However, neither side was injured. At that time, I was in Shenyang, and the Changchun County Government had not reported this matter. The Deputy Commander had telegraphed to inquire about the truth of the incident. It was the anniversary of the Grand Marshal's death. The next day, I asked Mr. Lin, the Japanese Consul General in Shenyang, to meet. Lin sent the Deputy Consul to meet with me, and each sent one person to Wanbaoshan to personally investigate the incident. After the investigation, they began to negotiate a peaceful solution. Our side withdrew the police team, and the Japanese side also withdrew the police. The Korean excavation work was temporarily suspended, and the excavation incident was handed over to the local authorities for legal resolution. Consul General Lin expressed his approval of this, and both sides ordered the withdrawal of the police. After our police team withdrew, the Japanese police also withdrew, but the Japanese used cunning means to replace them with twelve plainclothes policemen, each carrying a pistol to protect the Korean work. On the 2nd of this month, the two sides clashed again. I met with Consul General Lin and blamed him for the dishonesty of the diplomats. After our police withdrew, why did they replace them with plainclothes police? He said that he had recently received an order from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that the unfortunate incidents between China and Japan in the Northeast in recent years, such as the Liaoning Bridge Incident and the Wanbaoshan Incident, were enough to affect international sentiment and expressed deep regret for this matter. He also regretted the expulsion of Koreans from the Northeast. I said that I have always advocated peace and should be known to everyone. There is no such thing as expelling Koreans. The Wanbaoshan Incident is not an expulsion of Koreans. Otherwise, there are 600,000 Koreans in Jilin Province, both registered and unregistered, why are they all able to live in peace, and only 100 or 200 Koreans in Wanbaoshan are not tolerated by the people? Rice fields are not impossible to grow there, but they must be approved by the Chinese government and cannot forcibly occupy private land. Think about it, if the Chinese diverted water to grow rice in your country and forcibly occupied private land to dig waterways, what would your country think? Even if the mixed residence in the interior that your country advocates is achieved, you must abide by Chinese laws. The Wanbaoshan Incident has been investigated by both sides, and it is not difficult to distinguish who is right and who is wrong. Lin was speechless at this point. In short, the Korean's method of growing rice in Wanbaoshan was not approved by the county government, and the forced occupation of land to dig ditches was not in compliance with the procedures. The intense anti-Chinese sentiment caused by this incident is a big fuss over a trivial matter. All these circumstances have been reported to the Northeast Political Committee and submitted to the National Government for the record. As for the policy to deal with this matter in the future, the local authorities will still resolve it peacefully. Secondly, he said that Deputy Commander Zhang has recovered greatly and is in good spirits, but he is slightly thinner than before. He will be discharged from the hospital soon. My trip will return to Shenyang, with a slight delay, or I may have to return to Jilin. (9th)

Wanbaoshan Negotiation Case 64

Japanese Consul in Jilin-Changchun Repeatedly Makes Unreasonable Demands

Talking About the Recent Situation in Wanbaoshan Town

Victimized Chinese Farmers Issue a Proclamation of Proper Defense

Changchun Correspondence: After the Wanbaoshan Incident, the Japanese Consul in Jilin, Ishisha, based on the report of the Japanese Consul in Changchun, Tian Dynasty, went to our Diplomatic Office several times on the 3rd and 4th to meet with Director Shi Luben and demanded that our side send troops to quickly disperse the Chinese farmers who filled the ditch and disarm the self-defense firearms, so that the Koreans could continue their work. Director Shi replied that this time, the villagers of our country gathered to fill the trench, which was actually caused by the oppression of the Japanese side, and they were outraged by righteousness. The gathered victims, holding guns for self-defense, filling the ditch and leveling the embankment, could not be stopped. If the Koreans stopped working and the Japanese police withdrew, there would be a considerable solution. They dispersed without results. After returning to the office, Ishisha submitted a written protest to the Foreign Affairs Office at 10 am on the 5th. The language was extremely absurd. Just in time, the Civil Affairs Director of Kwantung, Tsukamoto, brought his secretary, Tomida Tokio, and nine others to Jilin to inspect the Jidun and other roads. For this case, he personally went to the Provincial Government and asked the acting chairman, Xi Qia, to find a way to stop the Wanbaoshan people from filling the trenches in order to prevent the occurrence of a second unfortunate incident. The Japanese Consul in Changchun, Tian Dynasty, also went to our Municipal Government three times on the 4th and 5th and asked Guo, the director of the Diplomatic Section, to order the Changchun County Government to arrest the leaders of the trench-filling people and bring them to justice. Guo replied that the Japanese police fired first this time, injuring more than a dozen of our Chinese people. The responsibility must be borne by the Japanese side. Please withdraw and punish the Japanese police who started the incident in order to appease the anger of our people. As for how to resolve it, we will wait for the Director of the Office to return to Chang from Jin before handling it. At 10 am on the 6th, the Japanese Consul went to the Foreign Affairs Office again and demanded that the people who caused the incident be punished. Guo Wan refused again and asked to withdraw all the Japanese police and troops first before negotiations could begin, otherwise there would be no way to stop it. The Japanese Consul left in anger.

The reporter recently went to the vicinity of Wanbaoshan to investigate and risked going to Majia Outpost, the scene of the incident fifty miles away from Changchun, to take pictures and met with Nakagawa, a Japanese police officer, and obtained the following results: The number of armed Japanese police has increased to seventy-three. Some set up tents to sleep in the open, and some invaded the residences of Wang He and Ma San surnames in Majia Outpost, using the dug-out ditches to build a two-mile-long trench, setting up machine guns and cannons towards the villages. Bombs and landmines were buried on both sides of the ditch, and carrier pigeons were used to communicate with the consulate barracks. In addition, dozens of police uniforms were used to order the Koreans to wear them to demonstrate to the villagers. At night, they patrolled for several miles. Under the protection of the Japanese police, the Koreans cut down the willow branches of the houses and filled sacks with soil to build dams in the river, which were more than a zhang high. However, the water was still far from entering the ditch. The water level upstream was getting deeper day by day. At Jiangqiao, twenty miles away from Majia Outpost, it was originally possible to wade across. On the 6th, the reporter rode a horse across, almost being submerged. Traffic on both banks has been cut off. The ferry at Majia Outpost has been occupied by the Japanese, and traffic there has also been cut off. Most of the villagers in the nearby villages have moved away. Those who have not escaped keep their doors closed during the day and do not go out. However, Nakagawa Yoshizhao, a Japanese police officer, told the reporter that there were no deaths or injuries in the incident on the morning of the 2nd, because both sides fired shots into the air. I was ordered by the consul to bring forty-seven police officers here to protect the Koreans. I only know my responsibilities and nothing else. The withdrawal of the police also requires orders. I sincerely hope to resolve it as soon as possible so that I can return to Changchun soon. According to Qu Xianglou, a representative of the farmers, the land in Wanbaoshan is all good farmland, and there is no fear of drought or flood. Now it has been destroyed by digging, causing hundreds of households to become impoverished. Therefore, everyone is of one heart and must persevere to the end. The farmers in the Wanbaoshan area are in a state of agitation, and dozens of villages have jointly organized a diplomatic support group. Their slogans read: "Our land, which is related to everyone's life and property, has been dug into trenches by illegal people and divided into two sections, harming everyone's work. We have repeatedly presented it to the government, but there is no solution. We have no choice but to decide for ourselves and implement proper self-defense measures. On the one hand, we will restore the original state for cultivation, and on the other hand, we will ask the government to order the illegal people to compensate for the losses. This is a public announcement." The public announcement of the victims of the Wanbaoshan farmland has four directors and thirty members of the support group, representing dozens of villages, and each has self-defense guns and farm tools as weapons, vowing to fight for land rights. When the police were sent to suppress and persuade, they were warned not to clash. However, if the Japanese dig the ditch again, a fierce battle may be unavoidable. (July 6)

Incheon Chinese Chamber of Commerce Reports Koreans' Harm to Overseas Chinese 65

Taking Advantage of the Wanbaoshan Case to Launch a Large-Scale Riot

Japanese Police Turn a Blind Eye to Overseas Chinese Being Harmed

All Overseas Chinese in Korea Have No Way to Escape

Beijing News: The Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Incheon, Korea, urgently telegraphed to Beijing for assistance, saying that Koreans have launched a large-scale harm to Overseas Chinese since the 3rd, using the Wanbaoshan case as an excuse. The text of the telegram is recorded as follows: "To President Jiang of Nanjing, Vice President Zhang, the Central Party Headquarters, various departments of the Executive Yuan, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and forwarded to various agencies and newspapers: Korean newspapers have been advocating the Wanbaoshan Incident, inciting Koreans to riot in Wai-ri at 2 am on the Jiang-ri. The Consulate General's Incheon Office has asked the local police station to strictly stop it and be responsible for protection. In the afternoon, the situation became urgent. The chairman of the Chamber of Commerce and the director of the office went to the police station again to ask them to prohibit newspaper instigation and take strict precautions, and telegraphed to the Consul General to order the Governor-General's Office to strictly suppress it to avoid repeating the tragedy of 1927. Unexpectedly, the newspaper still issued extra editions, intensely propagating, and the Koreans also distributed leaflets and held meetings everywhere. At 8 pm, two or three thousand Koreans gathered and launched a large-scale riot. The police's attempt to stop it was ineffective, and chaos broke out everywhere. When they encountered our Overseas Chinese, they immediately attacked them randomly. The Overseas Chinese either closed their doors to defend themselves or fled in all directions. All the Overseas Chinese shops and vegetable gardens outside Chinatown were mostly destroyed by rioters. Many Chinese were beaten and injured. The next day, the news got worse. The Overseas Chinese flocked to Chinatown to evacuate. The director of the office and the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, seeing that the riot was expanding and the lives and property of the Overseas Chinese were in extreme danger, went to the police station to ask the police to send armed forces to strictly suppress it, and telegraphed to the Consul General to request the Governor-General's Office to send additional military police to assist. The director of the office stated that he would assume full responsibility for the lives and property of our Overseas Chinese. The Governor-General's Office also agreed to send an additional 50 armed police. At 2 pm, the Consul General came to Incheon and went to the police station again to urge them to earnestly be responsible for protection. The director of the office replied as before. At 8 pm, more and more Koreans gathered, and the riot became more intense. The police had lost the power to protect. When asked by the police station, they said that there were not enough police to distribute. The Overseas Chinese were helpless and waited to die. The rioters, except for failing to attack Chinatown, wreaked havoc everywhere else. The situation was too horrible to bear. All the doors and windows of the Overseas Chinese shops were smashed, and the goods and appliances were destroyed and looted. All the vegetable gardens were also destroyed. Three Overseas Chinese were confirmed to have been brutally killed, and the lives of several others were at risk. About twenty or thirty people were injured but not fatally. The Overseas Chinese in various places who failed to escape were all escorted to Chinatown by the police in cars. It is estimated that the Chamber of Commerce has taken in more than 2,000 male and female refugees, and all the shops are full. At that time, the clamor of Koreans planning to break into Chinatown was extremely high. The Overseas Chinese had no way to escape, trembling with fear and in extreme danger. Please urgently ask the Consul General to make every effort to negotiate with the Governor-General's Office and ask them to send additional military police to rescue them. Another 50 armed police and 20 military police were sent. The Incheon police also carried weapons. The area of Chinatown is small, and the strength of the military police has been increased again. Although the rioters still gathered that night, they finally did not dare to break in. The Overseas Chinese were spared from disaster. However, two vegetable gardens were burned by them. It is difficult to predict whether this place will gradually calm down in the future and whether it will not spread to other places. It has been found that there are no less than several million Koreans living in our three northeastern provinces. There are good and bad people mixed in. It is inevitable that incidents will occur. The two governments will resolve it. If the people retaliate against each other, there will be no end. Since 1927, the Koreans have launched a large-scale riot under the pretext of our country's oppression of Korean Qiaos. It has only been more than three years since then, and the unresolved case has been repeated, and the tragedy has been several times more violent than before. The police station has repeatedly promised to provide full protection, but they are unwilling to take precautions in advance, and they have no sufficient power to stop it temporarily. They will only increase their efforts to strictly prevent it after the Overseas Chinese have been brutally poisoned by rioters. It is difficult to understand what the situation is. In this situation, if our Overseas Chinese in Korea do not have considerable guarantees, there is really no place for them to stand. The only way is to withdraw from Korea altogether. Please quickly find a way to protect them. The Incheon Chinese Chamber of Commerce bows."

Attached Report: It has been reported by telephone and extra edition from Zhennampo that all the Chinese merchants in Pyongyang have been wiped out, the houses have been burned, more than 30 people have died, and countless people have been injured. It has also been heard that the rioters have news of attacking Incheon Chinatown, and the situation is extremely critical. Please rescue them quickly.

The Legislative Yuan's 150th Meeting 66

Passed the Organizational Charter of the International Trade Bureau

The Legislative Yuan held its 150th meeting this morning (the 11th) at 8:00 AM. The attending committee members included Luo Ding, Shi Shangkuan, Zhang Zhihan, Lu Zhonglin, Liu Kejun, Zhu Luhe, Li Shuhua, Zhu Hezhong, Xi Chaojun, Liu Jingxin, Peng Yangguang, Tao Xuan, Lü Zhiyi, Lin Bin, Shi Weihuan, Fang Juehui, Wei Huai, Liu Shishun, Feng Zhaoyi, Enke Batu, Huang Youchang, Zhou Wei, Ma Yinchu, Lou Tongsun, Wang Yongbin, Liu Jixue, Zhu Jingsong, and others, totaling twenty-seven members. The meeting was chaired by Acting President Shao Yuanchong. Items for discussion included: (1) Examining the Organizational Charter of the Central Mint. Resolution: Referred to the Legislative Committee for review. (2) Examining the Organizational Charter of the Hangzhou Mint. Resolution: Referred to the Legislative Committee for review. (3) The Legislative Committee, in conjunction with the Economic Committee, reported on the examination of the Organizational Charter of the International Trade Bureau. Resolution: Amended and passed. (4) The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Yuan reported on the examination and approval of the agreement on the treatment of Chinese nationals going to Nicaragua and its annexes. Resolution: Referred back to the Foreign Affairs Committee for re-examination.

The Legislative Yuan Resolves to Re-examine the Sino-Nicaraguan Agreement 67

Previously, due to Nicaragua's promulgation of immigration laws with harsh treatment of overseas Chinese, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs specially dispatched Consul General Li Shizhong to negotiate with the Nicaraguan government for cancellation. Consequently, a draft agreement on the treatment of Chinese nationals going to Nicaragua was negotiated by both parties. In the annex to the draft, the Nicaraguan side declared: (1) The fifth clause of the Immigration Law of May 5, 1930, concerning the prevention of Chinese entry, will be abolished. Once passed by the Nicaraguan Congress, the agreement signed today will take effect before the exchange of ratifications. (2) The future formal treaty of commerce and navigation between China and Nicaragua will not be bound by this agreement. The content of the agreement involves our side voluntarily restricting the number of Chinese entering Nicaragua, with twelve articles stipulated. The first article stipulates that Chinese nationals enjoy the same treatment as nationals of other countries. Based on this article, all unequal and harsh treatments can be canceled. Articles two, three, and four indicate the method of voluntary restriction, limiting the number of overseas Chinese going to Nicaragua to fifteen per year. However, wives and minor children can enter freely. Articles six and seven concern the procedures for overseas Chinese traveling in transit. Article eight allows for the replenishment of vacancies when overseas Chinese die or return to their country. After the above agreement was submitted to the Yuan by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and thoroughly studied by the Central Political Council, the Central Political Council added the tenth article: "When Nicaraguan people come to China, they should be handled in accordance with the above articles of this agreement." It was then submitted by the Central Political Council to the National Government and forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. At the 147th plenary session of the Yuan, it was resolved to refer it to the Foreign Affairs Committee for review. After the committee met and reviewed it, they considered it approvable and submitted it to the 150th plenary session on the 11th. After Lou Tongsun of the Foreign Affairs Committee reported on the review process, it was submitted to the committees for discussion. The second reading then began. After the second reading, Committee Member Lü Zhiyi stood up and opposed the approval of the agreement, stating that the content of the agreement was absolutely unequal. Nicaragua is a small country, and our country is accommodating this unequal treaty for the benefit of only fifteen people per year. This violates the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen and sets a precedent for other countries to follow, making it even more difficult for Chinese to go abroad. Fang Juehui continued to speak, believing that the agreement should not be passed. Restrictions such as good conduct, sound health, and economic independence in Article Two mean that the Nicaraguan side can restrict the entry of Chinese people at any time, and this article reveals more of our own shortcomings. Furthermore, foreigners coming to China have no restrictions, arriving in groups of thousands, and there is no greater inequality than this. Lou Tongsun explained that although the number of Chinese going to Nicaragua is limited to fifteen, Article Five

Page 12

does not include family members (wives and minor children) entering the country, and the number of people who can be replenished in Article Eight is not small. If it is believed that not approving the agreement means preparing not to send anyone, that is fine. However, the 600 overseas Chinese currently in Nicaragua should also be taken into consideration. Furthermore, the Central Political Council has already added Article Ten, stipulating that Nicaraguans coming to China should abide by the agreement. Lü Zhiyi stood up again and stated that the provisions of Article Ten should have been explained under Articles Two and Three instead of being listed separately. We would rather suffer losses than have this unequal agreement. Shi Weihuan stated that Nicaragua is not the only country currently restricting Chinese immigration. The United States, Mexico, and others are also doing so. If countries follow suit and restrict Chinese immigration, then Chinese people will have no way out. The regulations on economic independence, etc., are even more inappropriate, because Chinese farmers and businessmen who are independent do not need to go abroad to do hard labor. Luo Ding said that although this agreement only concerns China and Nicaragua, it has a significant impact on the future of Chinese people going abroad. Nicaragua's harsh immigration laws can be ignored or protested through diplomatic channels for cancellation, without the need to conclude an unequal agreement to bind ourselves. He advocated not passing it. At this point, President Shao said that the meaning of the first article of the agreement is good, treating people equally, but the second and third articles restrict the number of people, which contradicts itself. Although the tenth article stipulates that Nicaraguans entering China should abide by the articles of this agreement, the ninth article states that this agreement should not prejudice the application of laws and regulations applicable to foreigners in general in Nicaragua, which is also contradictory. The atmosphere in the room was quite tense as the discussion reached this point. Zhou Wei, a member of the Foreign Affairs Committee (and also a member of the Treaty Committee of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs), stood up and advocated for a closed-door meeting, prohibiting audience members. Before the committee members could pay attention, Zhang Zhihan spoke, stating that this agreement was specifically designed to restrict Chinese people, and it would be difficult to deal with if other countries followed suit. Furthermore, the rights of fifteen people are not important to the 400 million people in the country. The criticism of our people in Article Three means that anyone can be difficult, and it should not be passed. Zhou Wei stood up for the second time, requesting a closed-door meeting. Ma Yinchu opposed it, believing that national politics should be open in principle and can be open. Lü Zhiyi stood up again and stated that if this agreement is passed and ratified, it will become a final decision and cannot be reversed or amended, and there will be no way to improve harsh treatments. Zhou Wei said that the annex states that the harsh immigration laws can be canceled after being passed by the Nicaraguan Congress, and we should take advantage of this point. Wang Yongbin said that in that case, we can refer it for re-examination. If they pass it first and abolish the immigration laws, it may not be a problem whether our side passes it or not. Zhang Zhihan spoke, disapproving of this method. This case does not need to be shelved, and the agreement should be rejected. Since we do not want fifteen people to go to Nicaragua, why should we wait for them to indirectly cancel the immigration laws? Liu Shishun spoke, asking to pay attention to the relief measures for the 600 overseas Chinese currently in Nicaragua. Shao Yuanchong spoke, stating that the agreement has many shortcomings and has been discussed for a long time. There are two main opinions: one is to amend it, and the other is to reject it. The method of amendment is that it can be referred for re-examination. If they pass it first and abolish the immigration laws, the Central Political Council will report, present the opinions of the committee members, and the Central Political Council will order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to earnestly negotiate amendments with the Nicaraguan side. When the amendments are sent, they will be submitted to the Foreign Affairs Committee together. The committee members had no objection to Shao's proposal and resolved to refer the Sino-Nicaraguan agreement back to the Foreign Affairs Committee for re-examination.

Recent Banditry and Mutiny in Shanxi Province 68

Bandit Troubles Reported Repeatedly Near the Provincial Capital

Another Mutiny by Garrison Troops in Pingding

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Xuan Army has been undergoing roll call verifications by representatives of the Deputy Commander's Office for days, and it is expected to be completed soon. Fu Zhan Kui, accompanied by Hu Jiesan, Director of Sun Dianying's Office in Pingding, arrived in Bing yesterday. It is said that Fu's visit is on behalf of Zhang Xueliang to comfort the generals and report on Zhang Xueliang's illness, as well as to inspect the roll call verifications and salary distribution of various units. He plans to stay here for two or three days before going to Jincheng and Yuncheng to comfort Song Zheyuan, Pang Bingxun, Sun Dianying, and others. In addition, the roll call verification representatives previously dispatched by the Deputy Commander's Office, except for Li Linshu, Ma Junwu, and Wang Zhizhong, who remain in Bing, are still conducting roll call verifications in various counties. Amidst these roll call verifications, an extremely unfavorable phenomenon has been discovered: conscription is rampant everywhere. Previously, this bad phenomenon only existed in southern Shanxi, but recently it has also appeared in Yucheng, Qixian, and other places near the provincial capital. As for bandit troubles, they have become increasingly serious lately. In Yongji, Zhongyang, Hongdong, Zhaocheng, Xixian, and various places along the Jinnan Railway, bandit cases have occurred repeatedly. The ransoms demanded range from three to two thousand yuan to as much as three to five million yuan. As a result, society is extremely uneasy. The people in Zhongyang have abandoned their homes and sought refuge in deep mountains and valleys due to the disturbances caused by bandits. Communist Party leaflets and declarations have also been repeatedly discovered in the provincial capital recently. If the Shanxi authorities do not take precautions against these multi-disaster-stricken situations, the bleak future will be unbearable. Regarding the mutiny of the garrison troops, news from Pingding stated that two battalions of a certain regiment stationed in the county town suddenly mutinied at 8:00 PM on the 4th after a heavy rain. At about 10:00 PM, they surrounded the county government and opened the prison. When surrounding the county government, the company commander of the fifth company of the regiment was killed by the mutineers for allegedly informing the county police chief of the situation. A platoon leader and a soldier were also killed. The mutiny was subsequently suppressed by the remaining troops, and fortunately, it did not affect the market. The mutineers left Qingfengkou in the southeast of Mengxian and headed towards Pingxing, which belongs to Hebei. The area is currently under strict guard. (July 7)

Quick Dispatch from Wuhu 69

The 9th was the 5th anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's Northern Expedition Pledge Rally. All sectors held a commemorative meeting at the county party headquarters, with hundreds of people attending. Party Secretary Zhang Shuye chaired the meeting and gave a speech commemorating the pledge, stressing the need to ensure peaceful unification. All industries took a day off, hung flags, and celebrated.

Shanghai-Hankou airplanes used to have a stop in Wuhu for passenger and mail transport, which was convenient for merchants and travelers. However, recently, due to the opening of the Wanxian station, the airplanes no longer stop in Wuhu for the convenience of navigation. The Wuhu station office was officially closed yesterday.

The Taiping Fellow Association here recently received a telegram from Taiping County stating that the bandit situation near Taiping is huge. The bandit force is the entire force of Li Xiu, and there is a plan to attack Gantang. The county town has telegraphed the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs nearby, requesting them to send troops to assist and order the neighboring counties of Qingyang and Shitai to block them.

The county party headquarters resolved to send a telegram to the central government requesting the cessation of the French investigation team's advancement and the recall of the team leader, Chu Minyi, to avoid insulting national sovereignty.

Since the past ten days, Wuhu has been experiencing incessant rain, and low-lying areas have become swamps. Areas like Fenglin and other villages in the four districts were breached by water, and other areas such as Baisha, Zhenghe, and the villages along the river are also in extreme danger. Stakes and wood are being used day and night to rescue them, and new dikes and embankments of Xintang Lake are being dug and destroyed to drain the water.

Representatives from all sectors held a meeting at the county chamber of commerce, stating that too many telephone lines are damaged and urgently need to be replaced. However, the telephone bureau does not have these funds. It was resolved that telephone users will borrow and advance 4,800 yuan to be used to replace the lines, which will be deducted from monthly bills. A report will be jointly submitted to the Ministry of Communications by the public security bureau, county government, and county chamber of commerce for record. (9th)

Jiangsu Provincial Party Department Requests Serious Protest Against the Wanpaoshan Incident 70

The Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee issued a telegram the day before yesterday requesting the central government to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to seriously protest against the Wanpaoshan incident. The original text is as follows: Nanjing Central Executive Committee: It has been found that the southward and eastward invasion policies of Japanese imperialism have been rejected by Britain and the United States, so they are focusing on northward expansion to realize their so-called continental policy. For more than ten years, they have repeatedly disturbed our northeast border and repeatedly committed atrocities, which can be seen as clear evidence of their desperate attempts to use force to invade our three eastern provinces and Mongolia and realize their continental policy. Recently, in the Wanpaoshan incident, Japanese police shot and killed our compatriots, and Japanese imperialists instigated Koreans in Pyongyang, Incheon, and other places in the Korean border to carry out riots against our overseas Chinese. The loss of life and property of our compatriots in Korea is beyond description. The tragic scene of people running for their lives and seeking to avoid death cannot be fully described in words. To this day, they have not stopped their atrocities. The Japanese imperialists' atrocities are the initial step in implementing their policy of military invasion of Manchuria and Mongolia. The seriousness of the nature is even greater than the Jinan Massacre. If we do not negotiate seriously, the consequences are unimaginable. We hereby telegraphically request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest as soon as possible, with the aim of achieving compensation, punishing the murderers, apologizing, and guaranteeing that similar incidents will not occur again in the future, and actively preventing their policy of aggression, in order to uphold justice and protect public rights. The urgency of the telegram is overwhelming. The Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang kowtows with dust.

Wuxi

Three Robbery Cases Reported in One Day 73

Recently, robbery cases have been on the rise in both urban and rural areas. Although detectives have been dispatched to investigate separately, few cases have been solved. Yesterday alone, three robbery cases were reported, which is a hidden concern for the future of public safety. The details are as follows: (1) In Xiyangqiao, an area bordering Wuxi City, a boat has been traveling daily between urban and rural areas. The day before yesterday, it was traveling from Xiyangqiao to Wuxi. When the boat passed the Hu Hui Bridge River at 10:00 PM, a pirate ship suddenly appeared from the Kan Zhuang Dangwai River. There were sixteen or seventeen pirates, each armed with long guns and short knives, who swarmed onto the boat and searched it at will. None of the dozen or so passengers were spared. After about an hour, they took the stolen goods and left. Upon checking afterwards, it was found that the Tianyixiang consignment had been robbed of 300 yuan, the boat owner and crew had lost 300 yuan, and the passengers had lost more than 100 yuan. In addition, dozens of pieces of ocean and general goods, mosquito nets, quilts, and clothing were stolen, as well as 1.5 taels of gold jewelry, totaling about 1,000 yuan. (2) At the home of villager Shen Peizhi in Lujianxia, at the foot of Longwang Mountain in the 12th District (Kaihua Township) of the county, more than a dozen bandits suddenly arrived at 12:00 PM the night before last, climbed over the high walls, and searched for about half an hour before leaving, resulting in a loss of about 200 yuan. The wife of Shen Peizhi's eldest son, Xiqing, was severely beaten. (3) In the Zhumiao village near Jingyun Zhoujing Port, Jin Zhuting's grocery store, which also served as a postal agency, was approached by several bandits at about 10:00 PM the night before last, who knocked on the door under the pretext of shopping. Jin Cai knew something was wrong and refused to open the door. The bandits then fired guns to intimidate him. Jin quickly rang the alarm, alarming the military police stationed at the parking station, who went to pursue them. The bandits then fled.

Fixed Amount of Business Tax Determined for Rice Industry 74

Previously, the rice industry had repeatedly petitioned the ministries and provinces, and united with all counties in the province to advocate that rice is a daily necessity for the people and that dental tile tax and donations had already been paid, so business tax should not be levied again. Subsequently, an order was received from the ministries and provinces stating that dental tile tax and donations are limited to the sale of bulk goods on behalf of customers, and that the sale of rice in stores is still subject to taxation according to tax rates. The Business Tax Bureau and the County Chamber of Commerce repeatedly negotiated with the standing committee members of the industry, and through great persuasion, the entire industry agreed to pay an annual business tax of 4,000 yuan, and limited the first quarterly tax of 1,000 yuan to be paid within the day as a final decision.

Court Investigation of Fisherman's Drowning Case 75

The patrol chief of the First Precinct directly under the Public Security Bureau, Zhu Guisheng, led police officers the day before yesterday to catch gamblers at Liu A San's house across the river from Huai Gu Bridge outside the East Gate. They arrested gamblers Sun Zhulin and others. The fisherman Zhang Koubaozi happened to be fishing there and, mistaking them for conscriptors, jumped into the river, resulting in drowning. His body was not found until the next morning near Dongshuiguan. It was carried ashore and reported for investigation. At 8:00 AM yesterday, Prosecutor Zhu went to conduct a legal investigation. The investigation revealed that the deceased, Zhang Koubaozi, had indeed drowned in the river. After the investigation, the family members were ordered to prepare a coffin for burial. The gamblers Sun Zhulin and others who were arrested were transferred to the Public Security Bureau by Inspector Yu Shuming of the First Precinct, and then transferred to the County Court. After Prosecutor Du opened the court for interrogation, he ordered them to be detained for further investigation.

Bandit Boat and Bandits Captured in Xitang 76

Liu Jihua, the second team leader of the second district of the local water police, under the command of team leader Sun Xiangfu, captured a bandit boat in Hongshengl the day before yesterday and arrested bandits Hu Guiqing and Li Sansan. He immediately led a team to interrogate them. Hu and Li confessed that they were from Jiangyin Beibei and had participated in a gang robbery of a Xitang passenger boat last month. Three original pawn tickets and an iron ruler were found on their person. Based on their confession, Liu's team leader prepared a document and submitted it to the district headquarters yesterday to await interrogation and handling.

Change of Commander of the Anti-Smuggling Brigade 77

Wu Hanzhuang, the commander of the Seventh Anti-Smuggling Brigade stationed in Xishi and concurrently the commercial patrol chief of the Xijin Salt Public Station, was ordered to come to Xishi in the year before last. He has been very serious in his work. Yesterday, Commander Wu was ordered by the Shou Bureau director to be transferred to the bureau for employment, and Chen Junxia was appointed to replace him in Xishi. As for the commercial patrol team, it will still be headed by Commander Wu.

A monthly interest of 5% will be deducted, and the county surtax will be used as collateral.

Yangzhou

Woman Who Has Been Barren for Ten Years Drowns Herself in the River 87

A woman named Lou, from the Chen family at No. 14 Beihexia, had been married for ten years and had not conceived. Whenever she heard that a neighbor had given birth to a boy, she would be so angry that she would try to kill herself, hanging herself or swallowing smoke, not just once. Yesterday (the 9th), upon hearing that a neighbor had given birth to a boy, she couldn't stop sighing. Her in-laws comforted and watched over her. Unexpectedly, at 3:00 PM, the woman suddenly took advantage of a gap and ran out of the entrance and drowned herself in the river. Fortunately, a water carrier noticed it and told the owner of the nearby beef shop to rescue her. As soon as she was rescued, she was unconscious. After being given ginger soup, she woke up. Chen and the landlord plan to go to Qiaoshu and talk to Lou's family to avoid future liability for loss of life.

Delivering Dumplings and Noodles, Loses Footing and Drowns 88

At about 3:00 PM on the 9th, a small steamer was parked outside the tax gate. Chen Tuozi, who bought dumplings and noodles, lost his footing and fell into the water while boarding the steamer. It was too late to rescue him, and he was drowned. It's a pity.

Rugao

The Bandit Xie Wu'er Arrested in the City 89

The bandit Xie Ma Wu'er from Lu Port, using the alias Zhang Mingfeng, had been hiding in the city. He was previously recruited as a porter and sent to Zhenjiang. Yesterday, he secretly returned to the city of Rugao. At Yanqiao Kou in the West Gate, he was spotted by Song Qingbai, a victim of his crimes, who recognized him. Song Qingbai reported this to the First Precinct. Patrol Officer Qiu led police to arrest Xie Wu'er. They found a return-to-origin road pass from the transport team and various symbols on his person. He was immediately sent to the bureau for preliminary interrogation by Section Chief Xu. However, the bandit gave a cunning and evasive confession, refusing to tell the truth. Later, Song Xingbai identified him, stating that Zhang Mingfeng was indeed Xie Ma Wu'er, also known as Xie Linyou. He recounted the burning and killing in Xiejiadian, Lu Port, in July, and the kidnapping of Song's wife for ransom, with Xie and Zhu Xiangzhi as the ringleaders. Many people in Xiejiadian still recognize him. Furthermore, the bandits previously captured by the Second Squad all confessed that Xie was involved in the burning, killing, and kidnapping. Song had been serving in the Second Squad at the time, so he knew the details very well, and there were records to prove it. Based on this testimony, Section Chief Xu ordered the bandit to be handed over to the county government for legal proceedings, as he had now been identified by the victim.

Massive Flood Disaster 90

In recent days, this city has experienced torrential rains, filling all rivers and canals and causing them to overflow. As a result, low-lying areas inside and outside the city have turned into a watery realm. Outside the four city gates, the water at the drawbridge entrances has submerged the city gate openings. Many streets and alleys within the city have deep water, making them impassable. Cars have stopped running, and navigation has ceased. Residents in low-lying homes are living in the water. Countless houses have collapsed. This is truly an unprecedented flood. The weather has not yet cleared, and the autumn harvest is a serious concern.

Urging Gongyi Pawnshop to Resume Business 95

The Gongyi Pawnshop in Puyuan, Jiaxing, suffered a robbery by bandits last month, incurring losses of over 100,000 yuan. It is currently sorting out its assets. The pawnshop owner, feeling the significant losses, has no intention of continuing the business. The provincial government sent officials to He to offer encouragement. However, many days have passed, and the pawnshop remains closed. Hurricane Causes Disaster in Wangjiangjing 96

In Wangjiangjing Town in the northern part of Jiaxing, thunder and lightning occurred around 4 PM the other day, followed by a hurricane. At the same time, there was a torrential downpour, with water on the streets reaching a foot deep. In addition, the patrol boat of the garrison patrol team was also overturned. Countless tiled roofs and walls were blown down in the town. For a time, people were shouting, and the sound of weeping shook the sky. The losses are immeasurable.

Shaoxing

Shaoshan and Xiaoshan Compete for Linpu Police District 98

The Linpu area is jointly administered by Shaoshan and Xiaoshan. After the establishment of autonomous regions, it became the Seventh District for Shaoshan and the Fourth District for Xiaoshan. Previously, police affairs in the area were handled by the Shaoshan-Xiaoshan Linpu Public Security Bureau. This time, due to the delineation of county boundaries and the reorganization of police districts, Xiaoshan established the Fourth Public Security Bureau, and Shaoshan established the Seventh Public Security Bureau. However, County Magistrate Du of Xiaoshan insisted on incorporating the entire town of Linpu into Xiaoshan County. Despite opposition from Shaoshan, he has not given up. He has now appointed Du Weiguo as the director of the Fourth Public Security Bureau of Xiaoshan County and ordered him to take over the Shaoshan-Xiaoshan Linpu Public Security Bureau. Bureau Chief Zhou Rujie, believing that the bureau was jointly administered by both counties and should not be transferred entirely, came to Shaoxing yesterday to request instructions. Public Security Bureau Chief Mo stated that Linpu, under the jurisdiction of Shaoshan, could not be incorporated into Xiaoshan. He had previously listed the reasons and submitted them to the provincial and county governments. Now that Xiaoshan County has sent officials to take over the entire town, causing public resentment, a fair decision should be made. He has submitted a request to County Magistrate Zheng for review and action. Meanwhile, Tang Zhonglin and over fifty other representatives of the Seventh District of Shaoxing have submitted a petition to the Shaoxing County Party Department, requesting that it be forwarded to the Provincial Executive Committee and then to the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, urging them to revoke the aforementioned appointment and order Shaoxing County to establish the Seventh Public Security Bureau of Shaoxing as soon as possible, dividing the administrative power to avoid disputes.

Anqing

Preparatory Headquarters Executes Unruly Military Officer 99

Zu Songquan, the former battalion commander of the Special Service Battalion of the Second Anhui Garrison Brigade, was ordered by Fan Xiji, the commander of the 26th Army, acting on behalf of the General Commander of the Preparatory Military Corps, to be escorted by the adjutant's office and the provincial government's guard regiment to the execution ground outside the North Gate at 4 AM on the seventh, where he was executed by firing squad. According to investigations, in February of this year, a mutiny occurred among the troops stationed in Lu'an, resulting in the deaths of many brigade and regimental commanders. Zu's unit was also among those who mutinied. When Chen Tiaoyuan went to Lu'an to inspect defenses, he appropriately punished certain military officers involved in the case. Zu submitted a letter of repentance, requesting to continue serving. Chen, finding it inconvenient to punish him in Lu'an, appointed him as an adjutant and ordered him to come to the province. He secretly telegraphed Fan, stating that Zu had allowed his troops to harm the people and that, upon verification, he should be executed. Fan placed Zu under guard upon his arrival in the province and executed him according to the telegram.

Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance Orders Counties to Prioritize Educational Expenses 101

Regarding the regular educational expenses for Zhejiang Province in the nineteenth year, after the Department of Education urged payment, the Department of Finance stated that many counties had not yet completed tax collection and remittance, leading to delays in provincial disbursement. As educational funding was urgently needed, all funds to be issued to schools were allocated to the counties, with instructions to prioritize disbursement from the collected funds. Schools receiving the notices have been actively going to the branch treasuries to collect funds.

Local News

Ministry of Education Temporarily Dissolves Labor University Yesterday 102

Orders all University and Middle School Students to Leave School

丨University Students to Register on a Fixed Date丨Middle School to Close

According to a report regarding the Labor University, since taking office, Wang Jingqi, the president of the National Labor University, has been working tirelessly to rectify the situation and gradually implement a system of half-day work and half-day study for the students. However, deeply ingrained problems have proven difficult to overcome. Social criticism suggests that Labor University students "neither work nor study" and are "arrogant and dissolute." While this may apply to only a segment of the student body, unfortunately, this segment wields considerable influence within the university, acting as they please. Their fundamental thinking is flawed. As demonstrated during a graduation tea party, one student openly declared, "All faculty and staff in the university are public servants of us students. We must supervise and guide them." As a result, any attempt by the university authorities to implement even slight reforms "invariably provokes blame." Trouble arises constantly, over matters both big and small. In April, the middle school division experienced an incident involving the expulsion of Mr. Yang Sifu, the head of the division. Yang, a graduate of Hunan Normal School and the Belgian Labor University, is known for his integrity and dedication, but his strict discipline of students led to a student-led siege, forcing him to resign. The university authorities proceeded with caution, sending three senior staff members to investigate. The investigation resulted in the expulsion of four students. These students refused to leave the university and instigated unrest, leading to a strike at the end of May and the presentation of numerous demands, including the reinstatement of the expelled students. The Ministry of Education sent Section Chief Dai Yingguan to Shanghai to investigate alongside Xu, the director of the Shanghai Education Bureau. Their mission was to address the unrest in the middle school division. On July 2, Director Xu and Section Chief Dai personally visited the middle school division. The disorderly and dissolute state of the students in their dormitories and classrooms was appalling, confirming the rumors. They immediately gathered several students from each class, inquired about the strike, and offered advice, arranging to continue the discussion at the university division the next morning. The following day, Section Chief Dai, accompanied by Superintendent Li, representing Director Xu, arrived at the university division and were greeted by President Wang. Suddenly, graduating students gathered and demanded that President Wang provide funds for a sightseeing trip, far exceeding the amount designated by the Ministry of Education. When the president refused, they gathered students from both the university and middle school divisions, broke up President Wang and the two representatives, and forcibly confined President Wang and Ministry of Education Section Chief Dai in Classroom 6, barricading all entrances. From 10:30 AM to 3:30 PM, they made various unreasonable demands. Police rushed to the scene to provide assistance. The police chief initially entered the university and attempted to negotiate a peaceful release, but the students refused. Later, a full squad arrived and were able to resolve the situation. During the confinement, the behavior of the students from both the university and middle school divisions of the Labor University was unrestrained. Their behavior, words, and actions were such that even those who were not present could imagine the scene. It can be said to be a great stain on the Chinese academic world, and requires no further elaboration. The university authorities have always advocated for sincerity in influencing young people, treating students with care and love, as if they were their own children. The students' behavior is deeply distressing. Upon receiving the report, the Ministry of Education decided to implement a fundamental rectification, telegraphing the university to temporarily dissolve. The university's announcement is listed below:

Announcement Regarding the Temporary Dissolution of the University:

This university was founded four years ago with the intention of implementing the Three Principles of the People through labor education, providing educational opportunities for poor youth, and nurturing leaders in agriculture and industry who are diligent, trustworthy, sincere, and respectful. Since taking office this year, the president has dedicated his efforts to this end, personally advising the students. Unfortunately, there have been repeated incidents of unrest in recent months. Some students have repeatedly violated university regulations, showing disrespect to teachers, engaging in siege and coercion, and displaying contempt and humiliation, again and again. Reason cannot move them, and understanding cannot be achieved. This is deeply distressing. On the third of this month, the aforementioned behavior occurred again. If this is not rectified, what is the basis for establishing morality and learning? How can we fulfill the expectations of the Party and the nation in cultivating talent? Therefore, in accordance with the Ministry of Education's order, the Labor University and its affiliated middle school are temporarily dissolved. (1) Graduating students of the university division must leave the university immediately and may not linger. (2) All students of the university division must leave the university immediately and await the university's announcement of registration procedures, to be announced at a later date. (3) The middle school division is closed. All students of the middle school division must leave the university immediately and await a qualification examination, to be held at a later date. Those who pass will be given transfer certificates according to their level. All of the above must be strictly followed. This announcement is hereby made.

New Initiatives at China Public School 103

China Public School in Wusong has a long history. Although there have been minor disturbances over the years, since the board of directors appointed Shao Lizi and Zhu Jingnong as president and vice president respectively last semester, they have been determined to make improvements, and the content has gradually changed. Donations have been raised to build a science hall, which will be completed in a few months. There are over 1,400 students. Zhu Jingnong recently accepted the position of president of Qilu University and could no longer oversee both positions, so he strongly resigned as vice president of China Public School. The board of directors was unable to retain him and instead appointed Pan Gongzhan as his successor to assist President Shao in handling school affairs. Vice President Pan has now agreed with President Shao to appoint the following faculty and staff for the twentieth year: Dean of Academic Affairs and Head of the Economics Department, Fan Zhongyun; Dean of Arts and Sciences and Head of the Literature Department, Xie Liuyi; Head of the Mathematics and Physics Department, Hu Yaomei; Dean of Law and Head of the Education and Sociology Department, Ying Chengyi; Head of the Political Science Department, Wu Songgao; Head of the Law Department, Dai Junliang; Dean of Commerce, Liu Nanhe; Head of the General Commerce Department, Zeng Bangxi; Head of the Banking and Accounting Department, Dai Lu; Head of the High School Department, Jiang Yingyong; Secretary-General and Head of General Affairs, Zhu Yingpeng; and Dean of Student Affairs, Tong Xingbai. It is reported that the course outlines for each department have been revised by the respective department heads, and each department will also appoint full-time professors to be responsible for guiding students in extracurricular research. The professors for each department are currently being sought. Special lectures will also be arranged, and renowned professors from other cities will be invited to give these lectures. According to Vice President Pan's statement to the reporter, his own affairs are very busy, and he initially intended to firmly decline the position, but he could not refuse due to the persuasion of various parties. He can only help to sort things out. In the future, the focus of running the school will be on increasing students' interest in academic research and extracurricular work. In terms of discipline and course content, strict attention will be paid to eliminating the old habits of laxity, so as not to fail the original intentions of the founders of China Public School.

China Organizes a Special Team to Participate in Sino-American-Japanese Swimming Competition 110

Xiqing is the practice venue

The Chinese Swimming Research Association was established in 1929. It now has over 300 members, all of whom started as beginners. Last year, it was not easy to hire volunteer instructors, so Yu Binqi personally guided those enthusiastic about research, and no fewer than 40 people were successful. This time, in order to improve techniques, the association is participating in the Sino-American-Japanese swimming competition in Xiqing. The competition was originally organized by country. However, the Xiqing Swimming Pool is not large, and it was feared that if the competition was organized under the name of the country, the scale would be too large, resulting in a small area for a large number of people. Therefore, the three countries changed to participate under the name of the group. Swimming in our country is still in its infancy. It would be difficult for one group to compete against the strong. In order to resist this, it is planned to assemble Chen Jinpei, Li Mulong, Li Chengyuan, Chen Jindai, Liang Guoquan, Xia Zeren, Xu Yaotang, Chen Chunji, Zeng Xuezhong, Ye Guihong, Jian Erming, Yu Binqi, and other strong players to form a Chinese special team to participate. It is also planned to invite Zhou Jiaqi, Chen Zhang'e, Peng Sanmei, and Ling Xitao to be honorary instructors. Shanghai is vast and populous, and there must be people who are skilled in this field. Those who wish to participate can register at the All-China Sports Federation on Tiwen Tai Road by the 14th, providing detailed resumes for active training.

The Future of Tennis is Bright: Cheng Yize Initiates the Youyou Cup Singles Tournament 112

丨Encouraging the Spirit of New Youth and Fostering Exceptional Talent丨

The Tournament Adopts a Round-Robin System

No one in Shanghai who talks about sports is unaware of Cheng Yize. Mr. Cheng has been promoting sports for many years. He has a considerable reputation in football, tennis, basketball, and handball. He is both an enthusiastic and a practical person. Recently, seeing that the progress of tennis in our country is slow and difficult to survive in today's fiercely competitive world sports stage, he initiated the Youyou Cup Singles Tennis Tournament to encourage the spirit of new youth and foster exceptional talent. This is a ray of light for the future of the tennis community.

Origin of the Association 113

Tennis has been popular in our country for many years. Although there are many people in our country who are good at it, there are very few who are skilled in it and can compete with famous players from around the world. Currently, the leaders of tennis in our country are only Mr. Lin Baohua, Qiu Feihai, Jiang Daozhang, who are all overseas compatriots who have returned from afar. There are no other outstanding talents in the country. The reason why our country lacks tennis talents is because there is no adequate practice. The progress of ball skills depends entirely on the method of practice and research. If a strong player practices with a weaker player, the weaker player can benefit from observation. If a strong player practices with a strong player, they can learn from each other in the same practice. If this continues, the weaker player will not always be weak, and the stronger player will become stronger every day. The more people who practice, the more they will gain. Everyone has their own strengths. They can take the strengths of others, make up for their own weaknesses, research each other, and discuss together. How can their progress be limited? The establishment of tennis clubs in Shanghai is limited to members in terms of practice. This is also the case for tennis players in Shanghai schools. Outsiders are not allowed to participate. Even if a friend is introduced to join, it is only a one-off thing. How can the opportunity to practice satisfy their desires? Therefore, there are those who join various tennis competitions to seek to improve their ball skills. However, many of the rules use an elimination system, and there are many who have only one chance to fight. How can this system benefit practitioners? It is not enough to talk about them learning from each other. Therefore, I initiated this association. The purpose is to seek more competitions to practice more, to progress with different levels of competition, and to connect the feelings of tennis players in Shanghai. Therefore, a round-robin system is adopted, and it is hoped that a group can be formed to study carefully and discuss methods of ball skills so that they can show good skills on the world tennis stage in the future. However, because the matter is a new beginning, it is not convenient to open it to the public for anyone to join. Therefore, a special letter is sent to invite you to sponsor and participate. I am very fortunate. Respectfully, Cheng Yize, President of Youyou Sports Association.

Rules Summary 114

(1) This association adopts a single round-robin system where each group plays three games, with each game counting as one point. The team with the highest total score wins the championship, the second-highest wins the runner-up, and the third-highest wins third place.

(2) All matches will be held at the association's courts.

(3) The balls used for the matches will be "Spalding" balls, provided by the association.

(4) The match schedule will be determined by drawing lots by the association and printed for distribution to all players.

(5) If a player is more than fifteen minutes late for a scheduled match, it will be considered a forfeit. The opponent wins three to zero.

(6) Match dates may not be changed. If a change is necessary, the association must be notified three days in advance. If the top three teams have the same total score, a replay will be held to determine the winner. The replay will still be three games.

(7) All three prizes for this event are donated by Mr. Cheng Yize, a member of the association.

Regular Meeting 115

Mr. Cheng Junye has obtained enthusiastic participation from Yu Tianguang, Liu Keng, Guo Qida, Tu Kaiyuan, Qian Yaobin, Wang Minshi, Liang Guanying, Guo Yujie, Mao Honggui, Hu Youcheng, Shen Baigui, and others. A founding meeting will be held at 7:00 PM on the 14th, and members of the press will also be invited.

New Plans for Jinan University Football and Swimming 116

Football Team Plans Overseas Expedition 117

| Expedition to the Philippines, Java, Singapore next summer |

| Large-scale plan takes shape |

The large-scale overseas expedition plan of the Jinan University football team has been rumored for some time, but it has only recently taken concrete form. The story is as follows:

Motivation 118

The motivation for Jinan's expedition arose earlier. Recently, a commercial inspection delegation from the Dutch East Indies in the South Seas came to Shanghai to inspect and visit Jinan. The head of the delegation, Zhuang Xiyan, is the chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Batavia. He stated that in order to develop Chinese culture and sports, it was necessary for Jinan to send a football team on an expedition. Thus, the idea of an expedition was greatly promoted.

Negotiation 119

Zhuang Xiyan then contacted sports, business, and press circles in Batavia, Java, and other places, who all agreed to support the plan. The Nederlandsche Handel-Maatschappij (Dutch Trading Society) offered 28,000 guilders for Jinan's expedition expenses. However, Zhuang recently returned from Japan and said that he was not satisfied with this amount and hoped for more.

Plan 120

The expedition plan is very large and will include the Philippines, Java, Annam, Malaya, Singapore, and other places. The number of matches will be over thirty. The team will depart next summer. Mr. Chen Zhang'e, the director of sports at Jinan, is currently selecting talent and providing ample training.

Great Britain defeated Czechoslovakia in today's doubles match and won the Europe Zone of the Davis Cup. They will now compete with the United States for the Challenge Round. Results of the British-Czech Doubles Match 124

Hughes & White (GBR) 6|4 4|6 6|4 6|2 vs. Mensel & Maleček (CZE)

Easy Victory for Great Britain over Czechoslovakia 125

After winning the first and second singles matches, Great Britain was confident in the doubles match. After taking the court, they won the first set 6-4. The Czech players suddenly put up fierce resistance and won the second set with the same result. Great Britain regained their spirit in the third set and played smoothly, resulting in a 6-4 victory. In the fourth set, they played casually and won easily with a score of 6-2.

Eleven-Year Reunion 126
