Free Talk

Words of Wisdom 235

— Songlu

The wise may think a thousand times, but are bound to make a mistake. It's far better to be a fool, muddleheaded and unaware.

To take a loss is to gain; that's why fools avoid lawsuits.

Fools may seem heartless, but are truly full of feeling. Their minds are simple, and so are their emotions. The feelings of a fool are genuine, not false; deep, not shallow.

Fools have their own kind of luck. This is often borne out by the facts. Fools tend to be rich, while the wise are often poor. The way Heaven treats people is truly strange.

Those who consider themselves clever are often the greatest fools. Those whom everyone mocks for being foolish sometimes display wisdom.

Only those who realize their own foolishness can strive and improve themselves.

Even the most brilliant inventors are often mocked as fools until their work is successful.

Fools are remarkably patient. They won't argue even if you insult them to their face.

Fools may be clumsy with words, but the wise are often blind in their hearts.

Fools have the keenest desire for knowledge, and they're willing to humbly seek guidance.

The wise study Buddhism with their mouths, while fools believe in religion with their hearts.

Fools are men of action.

Of the 108 heroes in *Water Margin*, the most foolish, Li Kui, is the most admirable.

The Strange Passenger Who Stowed Away Across the Atlantic 236

— Lü Bing

Recently, in America, a businessman named John Suning married his sweetheart, Ms. Wu Shi, in a blissful ceremony. The guests were gathered, and there was much talk of the amusing tale of how they had met. No one who heard it could help but smile. For Suning was none other than the strange passenger who had once stowed away across the Atlantic without a penny to his name.

Suning was British. As a young man, he had many fantastic ideas in his head. Ordinary people often scoffed at them, saying they would never come to pass. But Suning paid them no heed. He was in love with a woman named Wu Shi, but her family was stingy with money, and they could not marry right away. He admired the wealth of America and wanted to go there to find work, so he could fulfill his long-cherished wish. But when he applied for a visa, he was met with obstacles at every turn, due to immigration laws and passport procedures. Even the cost of the passage was too much for Suning, who had exhausted all his resources. Disappointed, Suning did not lose heart. He happened to see a ship bound for America, carrying cargo that included a large wooden piano crate, big enough to hide in. So he bought some food and drink, and hid inside it. The crate, which looked like a coffin, was stored on the deck, and no one touched it. Suning was able to cross the Atlantic in safety.

When he arrived in New York, the customs officials discovered Suning, and his story immediately came to light. Because of his strange behavior, the people of New York were amazed and took notice of him. Fortunately, a manager at a certain morning newspaper heard about the matter and admired Suning's ambition. He hired him to work at the newspaper. Before long, Suning's sweetheart, Wu Shi, came to America with her sister, Helen. They eventually met again, and were formally married. Suning now works for a sculpting company and earns a good living. He and Wu Shi are enjoying their sweet life together. It is not uncommon for people to travel without paying their fare. For example, the movie star Hossade once offered to work as a stewardess on a ship, and got a free passage from England to Canada. And Simpson was able to travel back and forth between America and Germany, on a long trip, with only eight shillings to his name. But the story of Suning's stowaway voyage is truly unprecedented. It is certainly a story worth telling by a reporter.

Vegetarianism 237

— Yingdai

Lately, the word "ism" has become the most fashionable term. All kinds of isms are emerging in endless succession. One cannot enumerate them all. But one has never heard of a vegetarianism. For human beings depend on food for life. Without food, one cannot live. Therefore, all people in the world consider food to be essential. Yet now there is someone who advocates vegetarianism. How can we not regard this as a strange thing? This person is named Herz, an Englishman. He is still young, and can starve for dozens of days without dying. He promotes vegetarianism and preaches it everywhere, sparing no effort. Recently, in London, England, he fasted for fifty days straight, consuming only plain water, cigars, and cigarettes. Yet his complexion has not changed much. He claims that practicing vegetarianism makes one's body stronger.

A Story of an Old Woman from Jiangbei 238

— Xiao

In a certain place in Jiangbei, there was an old woman named Wang, who was exceptionally clever. She was very skilled at collecting money. She was a sorceress. It is said that she became a widow at the age of thirty. She had no children and was very poor. She depended on her mother's allowance to live. Soon her mother also passed away, and the allowance stopped abruptly. Fortunately, there was a sorceress next door, who made a great deal of money. The old woman envied her, so she apprenticed to her and learned all her secrets. When the sorceress died, the old woman inherited her mantle, claiming to be possessed by a god, and divining fortunes and curing diseases for people. She also learned massage from others, which was quite effective. Her medical reputation even surpassed that of the sorceress. She practiced for forty years, and her name became famous far and wide. Those seeking medical treatment and fortune-telling numbered dozens every day. Although the old woman claimed that she did not care about money, the price of one treatment or one fortune-telling increased day by day. Therefore, she accumulated a great fortune. The old woman lived very frugally, wearing coarse clothes and eating vegetables, which she enjoyed very much. Those who invited her to their homes for treatment, no matter how far away, she would walk there, looking like a poor woman. When asked, she would say, "The god has instructed me not to disobey." In fact, she loved money as much as life itself and was unwilling to spend it. However, the fact that she had accumulated a huge fortune was known to many. Kidnappers had long been eyeing her. One day, a young woman came, with a sorrowful face. When she saw the old woman, she knelt down and wept, saying, "My husband is critically ill. All medicines have been ineffective. I beg the god to have great mercy and come to my home." The old woman felt compassionate and helped her up. She inquired about her name and address and said, "You go first. I still have several people waiting for the god to bestow a prescription. I will come as soon as I am finished." The woman thanked her and left. About an hour later, the old woman finished her work and walked there. When she entered the door, she saw a burly man with a fierce face. She did not see the young woman who had invited her. Suspecting that it was not the home of the sick person, she turned to leave. The burly man stopped her and said, "Are you the old woman Wang? Do not go." The old woman was startled by the voice. In an instant, she knew that something was wrong. She calmly replied, "Is there a sick person in this house? Then I should go and inform the host." The burly man stared at the old woman's face and said, "What are you talking about?" The old woman said, "I am the servant of the old woman Wang. A woman invited my master to treat a patient. Because I did not hear the address clearly, I was afraid of making a mistake and was ordered to come and ask for clarification first. If there is indeed a patient seeking medical treatment in this house, then my master will come soon after I report back." The burly man stared at the old woman's face again for a while and said, "Now that you know the address, why do you need to ask for clarification? Hurry and bring the old woman Wang here." The old woman nodded and turned to leave. Although her heart was uneasy, her steps were not disordered. After leaving the door, she began to walk quickly home. It turned out that this burly man was indeed a kidnapper, who had lured the old woman Wang into his trap. The bandits did not recognize the old woman. The bandit who recognized the old woman happened to be in the back room, the owner of this house. The burly man was the leader of the owner of this house. He thought that the old woman possessed a huge fortune and must be exquisitely dressed. Seeing that the old woman was wearing coarse clothes, she looked like a servant. Her words were also unhesitating, clearly not a disguise after being discovered. Moreover, the bandit was confident that he had not been discovered. Therefore, the old woman Wang's resourcefulness and composure were truly beyond the reach of ordinary people.

A Record of the Birthday Celebration at Dafengtang 239

— Weizhai Jushi

The brothers Zhang Shanzi and Zhang Daqian from Sichuan Province, disciples of the two great masters Zeng Nongran and Li Meian, are known in the art world, both at home and abroad, for their poetry, calligraphy, and painting. It is an honor to acquire their works. They enjoy a reputation of the times. This year, in May, Shanzi celebrated his fiftieth birthday. He recently returned from a trip to Japan and Korea with Daqian and their families. He composed a poem, expressing his lofty ambition to retreat from the world. The poem reads: "Fifty years have flown by. Difficulties rest by the sea. If the green mountains could be sold, a humble home would be no obstacle. In old age, my spirit remains strong. My poems become more refined. The lotus roots of Weitang are plentiful. I will build a home to serve my beloved parents. My horse is strong. It gallops across the borders. I can learn from the monkey to brush off my sleeves. The tiger can rest in my paintings. I leave my unfinished manuscripts in the East. I remember my hometown in the West. I am ashamed of my undeserved fame. When will I stop scribbling?" It is said that Shanzi served as an official in the East Province in his youth. When Sichuan was in turmoil, his mother preferred to live in Jiangnan, so he came to Shanghai. Daqian served his mother in Weitang, enjoying the pleasures of Laizi. Therefore, the *Book of Changes* says, "Do not serve kings and lords, but hold high your ideals." The *Book of Odes* says, "A good wife and a long-lived mother bring joy to the Duke of Lu." From this, we can see the happiness of the Dafengtang family, and we can also see that Shanzi's great works are lofty and unconventional, with a special origin. On the eve of his birthday, friends in Shanghai, such as Binhong, Danlin, Haoran, Duhe, Shoujuan, Yingbin, Changming, Zuhan, Chuqing, Yuhu, Shizi, Geyi, Gongzhan, Wanli, and Tianjian, will each offer their congratulations in the form of calligraphy and painting. His hundreds of male and female disciples, many of whom are outstanding talents, are also noteworthy. His female disciple Pan Yibin embroidered a five-character birthday poem by hand, displaying her miraculous needle skills. Her work is unmatched at the time, and it is a source of pride for the school. I have had the pleasure of exchanging letters with the two gentlemen. I humbly present a short poem, recorded at the end of this article, to offer a toast. How many talented people are there in the art world? Who stands at the peak of the mountains? The wind howls for ninety thousand miles. The plum blossoms have a longevity of a thousand years. In his spare time, he paints tigers and leopards. He boasts about his straw sandals. He records his grand tour to the sea. The brothers are both immortals. (A humble reply)

Random Musings on Korea (3) 240

— Ji Ping

There are quite a few Korean youths studying in Europe, America, and China. They are unwilling to be dominated and humiliated in their own country and can only seek development abroad. However, unfortunately, even if they succeed in their studies, they are still constrained by the situation and cannot return home. Even if they do, there is no use for their knowledge. How can this be? Presumably, those who return from overseas have, needless to say, advanced ideas and broad knowledge. When they think about how other countries are rich and powerful, they feel that everything about themselves is lagging behind. They cannot bear to see it, and their words and actions will always reveal attitudes of disappointment, grief, and resistance. Japanese secret agents pay the closest attention to their actions. When they enter the country, they are already secretly monitored. As soon as you have any expression similar to propaganda, it is immediately reported to the police station, who will charge them with a crime called "thought crime" and arrest them. Imprisonment for three months, five months, or even three years or two years is indefinite. This situation has long been unbearable for Korean students. Secondly, relatively subservient students, although they can be free, find it difficult to make a living. The Japanese are wary of them rebelling or starting a revolution, so they bury their talents. There was an industrialist who returned from Germany who could not find a job. The government directed him to work as a proofreader in a Japanese printing factory, with a monthly salary of twenty yuan. He reluctantly worked for three months but couldn't stand it and went abroad to make a living. Therefore, Korean students, once they go abroad, do not want to return home to live a hellish life again.

The highest administrative organ in Korea is the Governor-General's Office. Its organization is as follows: under the Governor-General is the Director-General of Political Affairs. Within the office are six bureaus: Finance, Legal Affairs, Academic Affairs, Police Affairs, Internal Affairs, and Colonial Industries; two departments: Agriculture and Forestry, and Land Improvement. In addition, three independent bureaus, namely Postal Service, Railways, and Monopoly, are also directly under the Governor-General. The officials in the Governor-General's Office are entirely Japanese. The whole territory is divided into thirteen provinces: Gyeonggi Province, North Chungcheong Province, South Chungcheong Province, North Jeolla Province, South Jeolla Province, North Gyeongsang Province, South Gyeongsang Province, Hwanghae Province, South Pyongan Province, North Pyongan Province, Gangwon Province, North Hamgyong Province, and South Hamgyong Province. Only one-third of the provincial governors of these thirteen provinces are Koreans, and they are all pro-Japanese figures. The real power in the provincial offices, in terms of police affairs, finance, and internal affairs, is entirely in the hands of the Japanese. They originally just put a high hat on the Koreans to win over the hearts of the people.

The Central Council is the highest advisory body in Korea, with only the right to advise and speak, but no right to vote. This year, the Japanese government ordered the Governor-General's Office to prepare for the initial stage of local autonomy and to organize provincial councils, municipal councils, county councils, and island councils. The chairman of the council can also serve as a local official. From April 1st, a grand election was carried out throughout the territory. In Seoul, cloth signs of candidate council members could be seen everywhere, standing at intersections. Most of them are Japanese. The qualifications for this election are based on property. As a result, Koreans only occupy six percent of the positions, and the power of the council is still controlled by the Japanese. Although revolutionary patriots loudly chant slogans of "national self-determination" and "Korean independence" (this is a secret activity of Koreans, which can be seen in publications, but cannot be shouted in public), it is still a pipe dream.

Rotary Club Story

??? (19) 241

— Xu Zhuodai

"Look; what do you think?"

"Shall we go to the station to pick her up?"

"No!"

"What's the point of dressing up like a clay idol and sitting at home?"

"There isn't even a full-length mirror in my house, otherwise I could see myself,"

After she said this, she went downstairs. Ziliang heard the sound of the door opening and knew that she must have gone outside to greet her. Ziliang anticipated that Ms. Ye Yunyu would arrive and knew that if the two of them started arguing, he wouldn't be able to write anything today, so he was trembling with fear, as if a great disaster was about to befall him. He wanted to quickly correct a few composition books before she arrived, but his heart was pounding, and he couldn't use his brain at all.

Suddenly, a burst of laughter came from the alley. Ye Yunyu had arrived. The two of them were in the living room, making a lot of noise. First, they scolded the rickshaw puller, and then Yue Ru told the nanny to buy noodles. Yunyu didn't allow the nanny to go. The three of them made a fuss for a while.

"You haven't eaten, you must be hungry."

This was the voice of the madam.

"I'm not hungry! I had a ham sandwich and a glass of milk on the train, how can I eat anything else?"

The lady, it seemed, had a good throat and her voice was still very loud.

But unable to disappoint the host's good intentions, the nanny went to buy noodles after all. After a while, the laughter started again. Ziliang listened carefully and realized that the lady had brought a pair of pressed ducks as a gift for the madam. The madam and she pushed them back and forth, refusing to accept them. After pushing for a while, the madam probably was afraid of dirtying her clothes, so she stopped pushing.

After finishing the noodles, they chatted for a few words. Suddenly, there was a sound on the stairs. Ziliang hurriedly closed the door of the garret gently. Oh no, the two of them came upstairs, but they didn't come to the garret to disturb Ziliang. They went to the front room. Ziliang knew that this was a courtesy that women always paid when visiting someone's home.

While Ms. Ye was relieving herself, suddenly Yue Ru pushed the door open and said softly to Ziliang:

"Why are you hiding here? A guest has come, you should go out and entertain them."

"I don't have time today!"

"She even asked about you, can you imagine how embarrassing it was for me? I had to say that you were feeling a little unwell today."

Sharp Decline in US Cotton Last Week 264

Government Report Favors Short Positions

Difficult to Increase World Consumption Next Season

A dispatch from New York on the 10th reports on the cotton market for the week, stating that after a brief surge in buying sparked by an agreement on the debt crisis issue, the cotton market softened and then sharply declined. This was because the government cotton field report favored short positions, and the new cotton crop's progress was also satisfactory. The eastern, central, and western parts of the cotton belt have all received ample rainfall, and the current temperature is also at its highest. It is generally expected that world consumption of US cotton next season will not exceed 12.25 million bales. Therefore, it is widely believed that favorable weather will lead to a bountiful cotton harvest. However, some also believe that the new cotton crop has entered a critical period, and many experts speculate that after the details of the debt deal are finalized, world commerce will improve, which may also increase global estimates for US cotton consumption.

North-South Goods: Prices of New Lan Bamboo Shoots Soar 271

The local market price of new Lan bamboo shoots was initially set at only 36 yuan, but then, because the Shanghai firm directly sent people to Zhangzhou to purchase the shoots, the price soared. Unexpectedly, it has recently risen even higher. It initially rose from 36 yuan to 45 or 46 yuan, and yesterday, according to a dispatch from Zhangzhou, it has reached 56 yuan, an increase of 20 yuan. This is not a good sign for the future. Although the output in various places is scarce this year, it is also necessary to consider the strength of the purchasing power of the sales side before determining the height of the price. Unilateral price increases will hinder future sales, which is not appropriate. The majority of the sales market for this product is in Zhejiang Province. The silkworm news from various sales areas is quite bad this year, so the sales of Lan bamboo shoots will inevitably decrease. Excessively high prices are even more inappropriate. Those in the industry should take precautions to avoid unexpected losses.

Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Sales Remain Sluggish 272

Yesterday, the local Shanghai foreign firm silk market was even more sluggish. American sales remained unchanged, and factory managers received no response to their telegrams. Current silk sales in England and France are sparse, and market sentiment is depressed. Yesterday, only 10 bales of white factory silk from Lianna and 10 bales of yellow coarse silk from Samsung were imported, and prices were flat and sluggish.

Hangzhou-Shaoxing Summer Cocoon Market Has Ended 273

The new summer cocoons from Hangzhou and Shaoxing have been on the market for more than a week. This year's summer silkworms, the early batches, were completely abandoned due to weather damage. The late batches were also not good, and cocoon production was still poor, averaging only 20-30% of normal years. The cocoon collection of cocoon firms in various regions was scarce, and the cocoon market has ended one after another. The highest price for improved superior cocoons required 60+ yuan, while the lowest price for local cocoons was 42 yuan.

Luxiang Zhenmei Tea Sales to Europe Slightly Active 274

Yesterday, the local Shanghai foreign firm tea market saw Luxiang Zhenmei green tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other regions, handled by Baochang, Tianyu, Xiehe, Jinlong, and other firms. The price of bud-picked goods opened at around 200 taels, and the price of ordinary goods opened at 140-150 taels. The market situation was not quiet. Needle eyebrow and show eyebrow goods also had some sales to French firms, but sales were not strong, and the market price was 2-3 taels lower. There were no large transactions for other goods such as Gongxi pearl tea.

Hardware: Military Factories Purchase Hardware Products 275

Yesterday's hardware transactions saw no major activity from customers or factories. The market situation was quiet. However, the business of the Nanjing Military Factory stood out and added a lot of color to the entire market. For example, 700-800 dan (unit of weight) of blue lead, 20 tons of red copper, 10 tons of white lead, 200 bundles of three-sheet black iron sheets, 15 barrels of white lead sheets, and other transactions such as tinplate, new lead wire, I-beams, and British steel plates were also significant. Prices remained unchanged compared to the market. It is said that the Hanyang Military Factory has also been quoting prices recently, and future transactions are also expected to be substantial.

Some People Maintain the Hardware Market 276

Recently, the hardware market has seen very few actual transactions due to telegram orders. However, after the prices were raised initially, they suffered a setback. The prices of tinplate, British and American flat white iron, new lead wire, flue iron, angle iron, tin, blue lead, and British steel plates have all frequently declined. Because the industry is aware of this, everyone wants to find a way to maintain prices. Therefore, yesterday, companies with ample financial resources all had the intention of maintaining prices, so the market may gradually improve in the future.

Kunhe Export Firm at No. 7 Huangpu Beach declares: The electric heating massager manufactured in France, exclusively managed by this firm, mainly treats rheumatism, back pain, neck stiffness, brain qi and muscle pain, obesity, weak stomach, constipation, swelling, blood stasis, insomnia, overwork, fatigue, boredom, dry skin, etc. It is divided into three types: for rheumatism, general use, and for obesity. Each unit sells for 28 silver dollars. It is widely used and takes effect quickly. Therefore, major hospitals and doctors in this city mostly use it, and it sells quite well. Now, in order to facilitate purchase by all sectors, it has specially entrusted Wing On Company, Sincere, Sino-British, Hua Ying, Da Hua, and other pharmacies to promote sales, and has printed Chinese and foreign language instructions for reference, it is said.

Sincere Company on Nanjing Road declares: Our company has newly shipped the second batch of the world's latest style straw hats from famous factories in Italy. The materials are superior, the straw color is pure white, the patterns are particularly delicate, and they have been processed by scientific procedures. Even if they are often exposed to sunlight, there is no risk of discoloration. Many people from all walks of life come to buy them very enthusiastically and are almost overwhelmed, it is said.

Mr. Wang Yanzhang of Lao Si Shun Chang Felt Carpet Shop on Jixiang Street in the French Concession declares: The Dongting Mountain scissors sold by our shop have been praised by buyers as being extremely sharp. Although the price of labor and materials is increasing, the original price will not be increased, in order to promote it, it is said. Lao Zhenghe Dye Factory declares: In order to give preferential treatment to customers, our factory issues 30% discount reservation coupons every year. This time, the issuance has begun, with a quota of only 2,000 coupons. Buyers have been extremely enthusiastic in recent days, which is quite prosperous, it is said.

Medicine News 296

A contribution from Boqian Advertising Agency states: Obutal is a new oral medicine for gonorrhea. After taking it, it can reduce and eliminate gonorrhea, relieve inflammation and pain, and is unusually effective for acute and chronic gonorrhea and gonorrhea in women. Moreover, the price is low, so it has been selling well all over the world. Major pharmacies in this city all sell it, it is said.
